***buikspreken.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:buikspreken.html>buikspreken</a> (47690)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Compound of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:buik.html>buik</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">belly, abdomen</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:spreken.html>spreken</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to speak</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:buikspreken.html>buikspreken</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>uncountable</i>)
</p>
<ol><li>ventriloquism
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl">buikspraak</span></span></dd></dl></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:buikspreken.html>buikspreken</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to ventriloquise</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li>Usage of conjugated forms of this verb <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> highly variable. The infinitive and active participle are relatively common. Indicatives are generally restricted to subordinate clauses. The past participle <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> very <a href = vnd.unilang:rare.html>rare</a>.</li></ul>

<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:buis.html>buis</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:buizen.html>buizen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:buisje.html>buisje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)

***buit.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:buit.html>buit</a> (4607)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>16th century, borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Low_German" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Low German">Middle Low German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="gml">büte</i>, whence also <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Beute</i> and eventually all other related forms.  Of uncertain ultimate origin; possibly a <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Celtic_languages" class="extiw" title="w:Celtic languages">Celtic</a></span> borrowing, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Celtic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Celtic language">Proto-Celtic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="cel-pro">*boudi</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">victory, booty, spoils</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.<sup id="cite_ref-2" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-2"> | 1 | </a></sup>  If so, related to the name of <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Boudica" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Boudica">Boudica</a>, a British Celtic queen.<sup id="cite_ref-3" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-3"> | 2 | </a></sup> <sup id="cite_ref-4" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-4"> | 3 | </a></sup>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:buit.html>buit</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>uncountable</i>)
</p>
<ol><li>spoil, booty</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:buiten.html>buiten</a> (299)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">buten</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*būtan</i>. Cognate to <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">but</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Luxembourgish" class="extiw" title="w:Luxembourgish">Luxembourgish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="lb">baussen</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/West_Frisian_language" class="extiw" title="w:West Frisian language">West Frisian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fy">bûten</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Saterland_Frisian" class="extiw" title="w:Saterland Frisian">Saterland Frisian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="stq">buute</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">without</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dutch_Low_Saxon" class="extiw" title="w:Dutch Low Saxon">Dutch Low Saxon</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nds-nl">buten</i>.

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:buitensluiten.html>buitensluiten</a> (25003)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:buiten.html>buiten</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:sluiten.html>sluiten</a></i>.

<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:buitensluiten.html>buitensluiten</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to shut out, to lock out</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to exclude, to shun</li></ol>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">bulle</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*bullo</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*bulô</i>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">bull</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bul.html>bul</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bullen.html>bullen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bul.html>bulletje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>, <i>feminine</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:koe.html>koe</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>bull <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">male bovine, or one of certain other male mammals</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li>surly person</li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<ul><li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">bull</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:stier.html>stier</a></span></li></ul>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bullebak.html>bullebak</a></span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">bulleboer</span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">bullenpees</span></li></ul>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">bulle</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">bulla</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">bull, decree</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_4">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bul.html>bul</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bullen.html>bullen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bul.html>bulletje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>great seal affixed to certain documents, notably <a href = vnd.unilang:charters.html>charters</a> from reigning <a href = vnd.unilang:princes.html>princes</a> and certain dignitaries</li>
<li>such charter</li>
<li>specifically, a papal bull</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3">Etymology 3</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><span class="maintenance-line" style="color: 777777;">(This etymology <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> missing or incomplete. Please add to it, or discuss it at the Etymology scriptorium.)</span>
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_5">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bul.html>bul</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bullen.html>bullen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bul.html>bulletje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>trinket, object of little value</li></ol>

***bulderen.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:bulderen.html>bulderen</a> (49830)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:bulderen.html>bulderen</a></i>, also <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">boldren</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*bulron</i>, further etymology unknown.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bulderen.html>bulderen</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to thunder, to make a thunderous sound</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to shout, to roar</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">buldering</span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">bulderlach</span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">uitbulderen</span></li></ul>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:bullock.html>bullock</a> (15448)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_English" class="extiw" title="w:Middle English">Middle English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">bullok</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_English" class="extiw" title="w:Old English">Old English</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">bulluc</i>, corresponding to <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">bull</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">-ock</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="ann-pos">diminutive suffix</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">boelekijn</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:bullock.html>bullock</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">archaic</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A young bull.
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1611</b>,  <cite><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Bible" class="extiw" title="w:Bible">The Holy Bible,<span class="q-hellip-sp"> </span><span class="q-hellip-b"><span style="font-style: normal;">[</span></span><span title="Conteyning the Old Testament, and the New. Appointed to be Read in Churches.">…</span><span class="q-hellip-b"><span style="font-style: normal;">]</span></span><span class="q-hellip-b"></span></a></cite> (<a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/King_James_Version" class="extiw" title="w:King James Version">King James Version</a>), London |  <span class="q-hellip-sp"> </span><span class="q-hellip-b">[</span><span title="Imprinted at London by">…</span><span class="q-hellip-b">]</span><span class="q-hellip-b"> </span> <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Robert_Barker_(printer)" class="extiw" title="w:Robert Barker (printer)">Robert Barker</a>,<span class="q-hellip-sp"> </span><span class="q-hellip-b">[</span><span title="printer to the Kings Most Excellent Maiestie.">…</span><span class="q-hellip-b">]</span><span class="q-hellip-b"></span>, <small><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/OCLC" class="extiw" title="w:OCLC">OCLC</a> <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://worldcat.org/oclc/964384981">964384981</a></small>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Book_of_Leviticus" class="extiw" title="w:Book of Leviticus"><a href = vnd.unilang:leviticus.html>Leviticus</a></a> <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://www.kingjamesbibleonline.org/1611_Leviticus-Chapter-8/14">8:14</a>:</span><dl><dd></dd></dl></div>
<dl><dd>And he <a href = vnd.unilang:brought.html>brought</a> the <b><a href = vnd.unilang:bullock.html>bullock</a></b> for the sin offering: and Aaron and his sons laid their hands upon the head of the <b><a href = vnd.unilang:bullock.html>bullock</a></b> for the sin offering.</dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li>A castrated bull; an ox.</li></ol>

<dl><dd><i>After that hit, there <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> activity in the <b><a href = vnd.unilang:bullpen.html>bullpen</a></b>.</i></dd></dl></li>

<dl><dd><i>If this team of consultants fails, I have another warming up in the <b><a href = vnd.unilang:bullpen.html>bullpen</a></b>.</i></dd></dl></li>
<li>An open seating arrangement where project <a href = vnd.unilang:teams.html>teams</a> can communicate openly with minimal effort.

***bullseye.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:bullseye.html>bullseye</a> (36257)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">bull's</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">eye</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:bullseye.html>bullseye</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">bullseyes</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">military<span class="ib-comma">,</span> firearms</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> The centre of a target, inside the inner and magpie.</li>
<li>A shot which <a href = vnd.unilang:hits.html>hits</a> the centre of a target.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href = vnd.unilang:darts.html>darts</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> The two central rings on a dartboard.</li>
<li>A hard striped peppermint-flavoured boiled sweet.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">nautical<span class="ib-comma">,</span> obsolete</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> Thick glass set into the side of a ship to let in light.</li>
<li>A hand-cancelled postmark issued by a counter clerk at a post office, typically done on a receipt for proof of mailing.</li>
<li>The central part of a crown glass disk, with concentric ripple effect.</li>
<li>A convex glass lens which <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> placed in front of a <a href = vnd.unilang:lamp.html>lamp</a> to concentrate the light so as to make it more conspicuous as a signal; also the lantern itself.
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1890</b>,  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Oscar_Wilde" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Oscar Wilde"><a href = vnd.unilang:oscar.html>Oscar</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:wilde.html>Wilde</a></a>,  chapter XII, in  <cite>The Picture of Dorian Gray</cite>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">He put on his fur coat and hat and <a href = vnd.unilang:went.html>went</a> out into the hall. There he paused, hearing the slow heavy tread of the policeman on the pavement outside and seeing the flash of the <b>bull's-eye</b> reflected in the window.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Great_Britain" class="extiw" title="w:Great Britain">Britain</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:slang.html>slang</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A £50 banknote.</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:bullseye.html>bullseye</a> lantern</span></li></ul>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Interjection">Interjection</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:bullseye.html>bullseye</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li>A cry when someone <a href = vnd.unilang:hits.html>hits</a> the <b><a href = vnd.unilang:bullseye.html>bullseye</a></b> of a target.</li>
<li>By extension, a response when someone <a href = vnd.unilang:makes.html>makes</a> an accurate statement.
<dl><dd>"<a href = vnd.unilang:did.html>Did</a> John steal the petty-cash?" "<b><a href = vnd.unilang:bullseye.html>Bullseye</a></b>"</dd></dl></li></ol>
</body>

***bultrug.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:bultrug.html>bultrug</a> (70726)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Either from <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bult.html>bult</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">hump</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:rug.html>rug</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">back</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> or a shortening of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">bultrugwalvis</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bultrug.html>bultrug</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bultruggen.html>bultruggen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bultrug.html>bultruggetje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> <i>or</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl">bultrugje</b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>A humpback whale (<i>Megaptera novaeangliae</i>). <span class="defdate">[from ca. 1950s]</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">dated</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A humpback or arched back. <span class="defdate">[from early 20th c.]</span></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:bultrug.html>bultrug</a></b> <span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic">m</span>

***bundel.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:bundel.html>bundel</a> (26304)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">bondel</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <small>[Term?]</small>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*bundil-</i>, derivative of <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*bundą</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">bundle</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bundel.html>bundel</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bundels.html>bundels</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bundeltje.html>bundeltje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>bundle
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hans.html>Hans</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:deed.html>deed</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:verboden.html>verboden</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:tijdschriften.html>tijdschriften</a> in <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:bundel.html>bundel</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:gooide.html>gooide</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:hen.html>hen</a> in <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:vuur.html>vuur</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation"><a href = vnd.unilang:hans.html>Hans</a> put the illegal <a href = vnd.unilang:magazines.html>magazines</a> together in a <b>bundle</b> and threw them into the fire.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>edition of collected literary works, often poetry
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl">Noura's <b><a href = vnd.unilang:bundels.html>bundels</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:essays.html>essays</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:werden.html>werden</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:verboden.html>verboden</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> geconfisceerd <a href = vnd.unilang:door.html>door</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:geheime.html>geheime</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:politie.html>politie</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">The essay <b>bundles</b> by Noura <a href = vnd.unilang:were.html>were</a> banned and confiscated by the secret police.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>any collection of products or services offered together
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:misschien.html>Misschien</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:moeten.html>moeten</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:we.html>we</a> internet <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:telefoon.html>telefoon</a> in <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:bundel.html>bundel</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:nemen.html>nemen</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">Perhaps <a href = vnd.unilang:we.html>we</a> should choose to buy internet and telephone in a <b>package deal</b>.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">collection of poems</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dichtbundel.html>dichtbundel</a></span></li></ul>

***bunder.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:bunder.html>bunder</a> (61518)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">bonder</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">bunra</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_4">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bunder.html>bunder</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bunders.html>bunders</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>A unit of measurement for area, a hectare
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl">hectare</span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">historical</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> An obsolete unit of measurement for <a href = vnd.unilang:land.html>land</a> area.</li></ol>
<hr />

</p>

***bunzing.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:bunzing.html>bunzing</a> (94794)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">bunsinc</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">bonsinc</i>, also <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">boesinc</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">businc</i>. Further etymology unknown, not found outside the Ingvaeonic language area. Probably a derivative of the dialectal term <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">boes</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">stable</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> with the now-unproductive suffix <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-ing</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">originating from, inhabitant of</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bunzing.html>bunzing</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bunzing.html>bunzingen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bunzing.html>bunzinkje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>European polecat, <i>Mustela putorius</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:die.html>Die</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:boot.html>boot</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:stinkt.html>stinkt</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:als.html>als</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:bunzing.html>bunzing</a>.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">That boat stinks like a polecat.</span></div></dd>
<dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonyms:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl">stinkmarter</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl">ulk</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vissen.html>visse</a></span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li>any polecat in general</li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>

</p>
<ol><li><span style="background-color:FFFFE0;font-style: italic;">(marterachtigen)</span> <a href="https://species.wikimedia.org/wiki/Mustela_putorius" class="extiw" title="wikispecies:Mustela putorius"><span style="color:green;"><i>Mustela putorius</i></span></a> <img alt="op Wikispecies" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b2/Wikispecies-logo-en.png/14px-Wikispecies-logo-en.png" decoding="async" width="14" height="18" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b2/Wikispecies-logo-en.png/21px-Wikispecies-logo-en.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b2/Wikispecies-logo-en.png/28px-Wikispecies-logo-en.png 2x" data-file-width="125" data-file-height="160" />, <a href = vnd.unilang:klein.html>klein</a> marterachtig, <a href = vnd.unilang:behendig.html>behendig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:roofdier.html>roofdiertje</a>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:burcht.html>burcht</a> (26760)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>With seemingly random addition of <i>-t</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">burch</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*burg</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-West_Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-West Germanic language">Proto-West Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gmw-pro">*burg</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*burgz</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*bʰerǵʰ-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">fortified elevation</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p><p>Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Burg</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">borough</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">-bury</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">burrow</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Danish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Danish language">Danish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="da"><a href = vnd.unilang:borg.html>borg</a></i>.
</p><p>For sense two, compare English <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">burrow</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:burcht.html>burcht</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> or <abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:burchten.html>burchten</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:burcht.html>burchtje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="Latn" lang="en">citadel</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">castle</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">borough</span>
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonyms:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl">citadel</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kasteel.html>kasteel</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:sterkte.html>sterkte</a></span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="en">burrow</span> of a badger, fox or beaver</li></ol>

<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr"><a href = vnd.unilang:bureau.html>bureau</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_French" class="extiw" title="w:Middle French">Middle French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="frm">burel</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">burel</i>.

<p>Related to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">burg</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">fortified city</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:burcht.html>burcht</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">castle</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

<ol><li>citizen
<ul><li><b>1988</b>, <i><a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>Het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:boek.html>Boek</a></i>, International Bible Society, <a href = vnd.unilang:richteren.html>Richteren</a> 8:9:

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2_3">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hamburger.html>hamburger</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:hamburger.html>hamburger</a></i>, from the German city <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Hamburg</i>, from the name of a fortress in the area, <i>Hammaburg</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_7">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
